308 Fan Ruimei, 311 Chen Jiajun, 313 Xiang Dawei, 326 Pan Yueying, 328 Wan , 345 Li Yukun, 347 Luo Zhigan, 351 Zhu , 353 Wang Lanyin, 363 Shen Peilan, 372 Bilian, 373 Fu Xiulan, First Day Summary of Men's and Women's Track and Field (Liao)

Long Jump Final

Of the 43 people in the long jump final, as many as 13 were absent. This kind of spirit is very poor. We hope that this kind of situation will not happen again in any sports meeting in this city. Yesterday's long jump final was still barely satisfactory. The four people who got the top positions all jumped over six meters. Wang Jihuai won first place with 6.22 meters. Li Lin also jumped to 6.20 meters. In terms of results, although it cannot be said to be excellent, having such results on a newly repaired and loose runway is not easy. Since the last heavy rain and water accumulation at the Dong Zhonghua Track and Field, the various runways of the field event venue have been uneven. A week ago, workers were hired to repair and loosen the original runway, and more coal ash was added. Although it was rolled frequently, it still could not be used. If today's triple jump is still held in the original location, poor results can be predicted. We hope that the venue department will quickly find a way to remove a thin layer of the loose material on top and then roll it again, so that today's triple jump and the 50-meter long jump in the next few days can have good results. In yesterday's long jump, during the third jump of the preliminary round, Zhong Lianji and Li Lin both had a score of 5.90 meters, ranking sixth. Zhong and Li each made a fourth jump to compete for the right to participate in the final. As a result, Li's luck was high, surpassing Zhong and winning the right to the final, and also winning the second place. In the third jump of the final, he once led the trend with a score of meters 20, exceeding Wang Jihuai. However, during the second jump, Wang opened the horsepower and jumped to a score of 6.32 meters. Li, who was also in the critical stage of the high jump, gave up the long jump and focused on the high jump. Wang won the championship steadily. Hao Chunde and Dong Zhaobin ranked third and fourth. Li Lin finished second. But in the eyes of the reporter, neither Wang Jihuai nor Li Lin are talented in the long jump. Wang's body is too heavy, and it is more suitable for him to practice heavy throwing. I am afraid that in another year or two, his body will become fat and he will not be able to maintain his current state. Li's body is too small, and although his elasticity is good, he suffers a lot and it is difficult for him to achieve special results. However, if Li can give up everything and concentrate on practicing pole vault, then his pole vault results will definitely improve. I don't know if Wang and Li agree.

Winners of the Discus Final

(From left to right) 1st Wang Jihuai, 2nd Luo Chuanxian, 3rd Chen Ruoxu, 4th Tang Xianzhou

Photo

Discus Final

The discus event has been progressing very slowly in Shanghai. Yesterday, this newspaper briefly mentioned it. Yesterday's final was enough to prove that what the reporter said was true. In such a large-scale sports meeting, only two people threw over 30 meters, and most of the other scores were around 25 meters, and even 22 meters. I think it is a strange thing. Although I expected that the results would not be very good, but the average score is so childish. The reporter could not figure out the reason, so I asked Mr. Wang Jihuai, who won the first place in this event. According to Wang, "The reason why the progress of the discus and javelin throw is slower is that practicing the discus and javelin requires a very large venue. When practicing, you must have a partner to help, otherwise it will be quite troublesome to throw back and forth. Therefore, there are fewer people who practice these kinds of sports in schools and in society, so the progress is slow. This situation is not unique to Shanghai, but the same is true everywhere in China. As for the average score of today's discus being particularly low, it is also related to the fact that the summer vacation has just passed and school has only been open for less than ten days. Most athletes lack practice, and the headwind also makes it difficult." The reporter suddenly realized after hearing what Wang said. After checking the roster of yesterday's competition, there were originally 23 people, but 5 people were absent. In the three preliminary rounds, Wang Jihuai ranked first with 30.80 meters, and Luo Chuanxian ranked second with a difference of 21 meters. The next were Fu Boming, Tang Xianhan, Xie Quanhe, Cao Yu, etc. In the three final rounds, the other players made no progress. Only Wang Jihuai threw 32.063 meters in the sixth throw, and the competition ended from then on.

Women's High Jump Final

The most interesting thing in yesterday's women's high jump final was the fierce competition between Ms. Zhu Wencheng, Sun Xiaoxia, and Li Shihui for third place. They raised and lowered the bar, and the competition was very fierce. As a result, Ms. Li was the first to be eliminated. Ms. Zhu and Sun continued to compete. In the end, Ms. Zhu won the fourth group, but she had exhausted her strength. In total, Ms. Zhu and Sun jumped more than eleven times to compete for fourth place. You can imagine the scene of the competition at that time.

Women's Long Jump Final

Among the 14 female athletes who competed in the long jump final, it was a happy event that three of them jumped over four meters on such a loose runway. There were also many who jumped over 3.80 meters. This is enough to show that the women's long jump event has indeed made progress in recent months. Among them, Ms. Qian Xingsu was the most confident. Except for the first jump, which was 3.99 meters, the other five jumps were all over four meters. In the third jump, she broke Zhang Pingxian's new Shanghai record of 4.30 meters set in the school sports meeting in the first half of the year, and ranked first with a score of 4.36 meters. Ms. Zhang Pingxian seemed to have regressed. Although she jumped over four meters in all three final rounds, her best score was 4.20 meters, which was 10 meters less than her previous score. I don't know if this regression is due to lack of practice during the summer vacation. I hope Ms. Zhang will work hard and set a new record at the National Games to win honor for the team.

Various Preliminary and Semifinal Races

Yesterday, there were over forty groups of preliminary and semifinal races for both men and women. The frequent malfunctions of the starting pistol mechanism were somewhat disappointing. However, the athletes' spirit was not diminished by this. There are a few things that must be said:

1. Starting Posture: A portion of the athletes have not yet mastered even the basic starting stance. Both their hands and feet are laughable to watch. Although their participation is commendable, they should also assess their own abilities to see if they are qualified to compete in such a large-scale city-wide sports meet. Otherwise, if one percent of the millions of adults in Shanghai participate in sports, the sports meet would last for one or two months.

2. Running Shoes: Without running shoes, even a naturally gifted athlete cannot achieve outstanding results in sprints. However, in yesterday's men's 100-meter and 200-meter preliminary races, two individuals wore leather shoes and rubber shoes, respectively, which was extremely ridiculous. Wearing cloth shoes is essentially the same as running barefoot, and participating in sprint races in cloth shoes at a prestigious city-wide sports meet is truly unsightly.

3. Absences: In yesterday's more than thirty groups of races, over one hundred and thirty people were absent, which is astonishing. Some say this is because no registration fee was collected during registration. I do not know if this is the case. The reporter is unsure.

Petty Details

The intense heat has subsided, and the refreshing autumn breeze has risen. Everyone is filled with energy and joy. On the roads, there is a constant stream of traffic, and the sports field is packed with people. This was the grand scene of yesterday's city-wide sports meet. The results of each competition are recorded in special columns. These trivial and miscellaneous details, however, have no specific category to be placed in, so a separate column called "Petty Details" is created to record them. It is written without any order or priority, pieced together from various sources, simply for the sake of liveliness.

▲ The Grandstand Assembly: There are four grandstands in the entire venue: the command stand, the sound stage, the various office stands, and the first-aid stand. The four stands are connected and adjacent to each other, one next to the other, which can be described as an assembly of stands. Climbing up the steps, the entire venue is in view. The autumn breeze caresses the sleeves, making one feel relaxed and comfortable. Therefore, the four stands are truly the best vantage points in the entire venue. Consequently, there are many spectators who cannot get onto the stands and sigh with longing at the stands below. Both ends of the passage under the stands are enclosed with iron wire mesh, with small doors for entry and exit. However, many people are still unaware of this and try to knock on the gates to enter. The enviable life on the stands is truly extraordinary.

The Command Stand Glimmers: The command stand is built with thatched bamboo and reed mats, high and airy, with good ventilation. Standing high above, one feels like an immortal. All the prizes donated by various sectors for this competition are piled on the stand. Shields, trophies, cups, and banners gleam with silver light, arranged neatly and orderly. From afar, one sees only the flashing light, constantly dazzling the eyes. An hour before the closing ceremony, the staff members busily carried them away. Many athletes in the field watched them go, surely wondering who would receive these items.

▲ Loudly Shouting (Boy Scouts Attention): In front of the command stand, there is an electrical sound amplification machine with two loudspeakers on either side. The orders issued from the stand can be heard clearly even by those standing far away. The starter, Shao Ji, has a loud voice and a dignified manner. When he shouts loudly, everyone responds. The phrase "(Boy Scouts Attention)" is his most common phrase. Whenever a competition begins, one can hear the sound amplifier broadcasting: "(Boy Scouts Attention, inspect the spectators and do not let them enter the field.)" And sometimes he shouts loudly, "(Boy Scouts are here to maintain order, not just to watch the competition.)" This seems to have a slightly rousing effect.

▲ A Glimpse of Female Athletes' Attire: Yesterday, there were quite a few female athletes participating in the competition. Their attire varied in color. Among them, the violet upper garments of the East Asia Physical Education College and the green shorts of the Liangjiang Girls' School were the most vibrant and eye-catching. The Wuben athletes wore white upper garments and navy-blue shorts. The attire of the Jinan girls was similar to that of Wuben, except that the blue of the shorts was darker. The green shorts of Liangjiang were trimmed with white stripes. During the races, these white stripes fluttered constantly.

▲ One Bread Shared by Two: Yesterday, there were about one hundred boy scouts serving in the field. The male and female members from Liangjiang and Shanghai Middle Schools were equally divided. Despite the heavy workload and limited manpower, they maintained excellent spirits. However, with so many spectators in the field, maintaining order was not easy. Their hard work is truly commendable. In the afternoon, staff members distributed bread, shouting loudly about bread as they went around the field. Before the shouting had ended, rectangular loaves of bread were already flying through the air. A female boy scout caught a loaf of bread and was about to eat it when a staff member shouted, "(One bread shared by two!)" Therefore, this female boy scout had no choice but to share the bread equally with her companion.

▲ Photographers Eating Dust: There were no fewer than ten photographers in the entire venue, running back and forth busily. However, during the women's long jump competition, most of them sat on the ground, forming a semicircle around the sandpit. Every time a female athlete ran and jumped, the photographers bowed their heads and pressed the shutter. The sound of clicking could be faintly heard. When the competition ended, they all exclaimed, "(Eating a meal of dust!)" This is because every time a female athlete jumped into the sand, she would inevitably kick up some sand.

▲ To Move or Not to Move: After the long jump competition ended, the photographers all requested to take photos of female athletes numbers 316, 348, and 346. The three women linked arms and stood side by side in front of the camera, holding their breath and not moving, waiting to be photographed. At this time, there were also people in the crowd taking motion pictures, vigorously cranking their camera. The photographers taking still pictures constantly shouted, "(Don't move!)" while those taking motion pictures shouted loudly, "(Move, move!)" Those who heard this could not help but laugh.

▲ Spectators Shouting "Bald Head": In the men's track and field high jump competition, there was a student from the merchant marine school, Chen Tianhe, number 35, whose high jump performance was very good. However, this gentleman's head was bald, which was slightly different from others. The spectators on the stands did not shout his number but shouted loudly, "(Bald Head!)" Whenever it was a crucial moment, the shouts of "(Bald Head!)" were incessant, and those who heard it could not help but smile.

▲ Hai Xing Cares About Jiaotong: At 4 PM, Jiaotong University and Soochow University competed in volleyball. Both sides were evenly matched, with skillful offense and defense. The spectators' spirits were greatly boosted. However, among the spectators, Hai Xing was most concerned about Jiaotong University. Whenever Jiaotong University was defeated, the female members of the Hai Xing team would sigh with regret. A sound of "(Ah-yo!)" was leisurely and meaningful. However, when Jiaotong University won, they would wave their hands and feet and cheer incessantly. After Hai Xing's shouts, the audience also showed great joy.

Luo Bo Cup Final Today: China vs. England

Around 4 PM at the French Club

2:30 PM: Mixed Doubles Final

Yesterday, in the Luo Bo Cup International Tennis Semifinals at the French Club, China defeated Portugal and England defeated Japan. The results were all straight sets. Today, China and England will meet again at the same venue to compete for the championship. At 2:30 PM, the mixed doubles final will be held first, with Canavero and Ms. Corazza facing Bu Tuo and Ms. Firth. Following this, the China-England Luo Bo Cup final will be held. This is also one of the most important international competitions in this tennis season.

Lin and Qiu Prepared to Win

Today they battle formidable opponents

Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai are two of China's top tennis players. Their doubles partnership is their greatest masterpiece. Yesterday, they defeated the Portuguese doubles masters Canavero and Tafolla, but their full strength was not fully revealed, perhaps waiting for today's final. Their opponents, the British generals Delve and Turk, are highly skilled and experienced, with a long-standing reputation in the tennis world. Today, Lin and Qiu are determined to win and show their prowess. The British doubles team's reputation is at stake, so they will not be easily defeated. A wonderful performance can be anticipated.

England Eliminates Japan

Result: 3-0

Delve 6-0 Yongsong

(Eng) 6-0 (Jap)

Turk 6-3 Okashi

▲ Strength Too Disparate: Delve has been in Shanghai for only a short time, but his reputation has grown rapidly. His skills are undoubtedly excellent. His doubles game is his forte, with unique skills. His partner, Turk, is a top-class British tennis player. Their cooperation is outstanding. The Japanese general, Tawarazumi, did not participate. Yongsong and Okashi, who played, are not all-rounders. Comparing the two sides, the difference in strength is too great. After the start of the match, the strengths and weaknesses were immediately apparent. England won two sets and two games in a row (a total of fourteen games), like a fleeting dream. The winners, the losers, and the spectators all had a inexplicable feeling. In fact, the difference in skill was too great.

▲ Japanese Change Tactics: In the third game of the third set, the Japanese suddenly changed their tactics, using high lobs to avoid the opponent's fierce volleys. This was effective, and they quickly won a game. Once the record was opened, their momentum gradually increased. Although England was strong, they could not do as they pleased at this time, and the situation turned into a stalemate. The score was tied at 2-2, 3-3, and so on. The Japanese fought hard despite the unfavorable circumstances, showing great spirit. In the end, England won the third set 6-3. The entire match lasted one hour, with three sets completed.

China Defeats Portugal

Result: 3-0

Lin Baohua 6-1 Canavero

(China) 10-8 (Port)

Qiu Feihai 7-5 Tafolla

▲ Easy Start: Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai entered the field, and the spectators applauded to welcome them. Then, the veteran Canavero arrived, and they warmed up with each other. When Tafolla arrived, the bell had already rung four times, and the battle began immediately. Lin and Qiu launched a head-on attack, gaining the upper hand first. Their natural coordination was both soft and hard. They easily won the first four games. Canavero and Tafolla, the doubles masters, had not partnered for a long time, so they were inevitably rusty. Moreover, Tafolla's offensive skills were not yet fully refined, so he made many mistakes. The Portuguese only won the fifth game. Then, the next two games belonged to China again. The result of the first set was 6-1, with China winning.

▲ How Difficult to Resolve: Judging from the first set, China could have played with their opponents at will. Unexpectedly, the Portuguese's form gradually improved, showing signs of a return to their golden age. They soon took the lead with a score of 4-1. Lin and Qiu tried their best to rally, creating a 5-5, 6-6, 7-7, 8-8 tie. In the end, China won 10-8. In the third set, China gained the upper hand first, making rapid gains, creating a 5-2 advantage. In the blink of an eye, the Portuguese rallied, winning three points in a row, making it 5-5. Fortunately, China worked harder and finally won the third set 7-5.

The National Games Will Not Be Postponed

Efforts Made to Save on Expenses

Nanjing, December 12th: Due to the disaster relief issue, various parties have advocated postponing the National Games. However, the organizing committee stated that it would not stop any preparations and would continue to actively proceed, saying that it would strive to save on expenses during the Games. The original budget of approximately 200,000 yuan has now been reduced to 120,000 yuan.

Recording the Second Zhejiang Provincial Games

Opened Yesterday

Yesterday was the opening day of the Second Zhejiang Provincial Games. The venue was the Provincial Stadium at the Meidong Gaoqiao Dayingpan, the same place where the previous National Games were held. At 9 AM, the opening ceremony was held. Chairman Zhang delivered the opening speech, the representative of the Provincial Party Department, Xiang Shirong, and the representative of the Provincial Government, Fang Ce, delivered instructive speeches, and Vice-Chairman Zhang delivered a welcome speech. The athletes took the oath, sang the conference song, took photos, and shouted slogans. Finally, more than 200 students from the Provincial Hangzhou Normal School Affiliated Elementary School performed gymnastics, and then the various sports began.

Triangular Inter-port Swimming Competition: Hong Kong Wins the Championship

Chinese Huang Zhenxing Fourth Individually

Hong Kong: 40 points

Shanghai: 39 points

Tianjin: 29 points

Two New Shanghai Records Created

In the three-day Shanghai-Hong Kong-Tianjin triangular inter-port swimming competition, Hong Kong won the championship with 40 points. The Chinese, Huang Zhenxing, accounted for 8 points, which was a great contribution. Shanghai failed due to the elimination in the 440-yard race, losing hope of winning the championship. In the final water polo match, they defeated Hong Kong 3-2, recovering 3 points, but were still one point short and relegated to second place. It was truly unfair. Tianjin participated in the inter-port competition for the first time and excelled in short distances, scoring a total of 29 points. Tomorrow night at 8 PM, a celebration banquet will be held at the French Club, inviting the three teams, officials, etc., in commemoration.

Important News

Municipal Bureau of Education Orders All Private Primary and Secondary Schools to Start Classes Immediately

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued an order to all private schools in the city that have not yet started classes, or have started classes but have not yet begun teaching, to start classes immediately and not delay on any pretext. The order states that the start dates for schools at all levels are fixed and have been announced previously. Now, according to the school calendar for the 20th year of the Republic of China, the start date for primary and secondary schools has passed for more than two weeks. It has been reported that some private primary and secondary schools have not yet started classes, or have started classes but have not yet begun teaching, which is a violation of regulations and a disservice to students and is highly inappropriate. Therefore, all private primary and secondary schools in the city that have not yet started classes are hereby ordered to start classes immediately and not delay on any pretext, in order to emphasize academics. If violations are found again after investigation, the schools will be immediately shut down. This is to be followed accordingly.

Local News

Opening Ceremony of the Road and City Exhibition Yesterday

Distinguished Guests Delivered Passionate Speeches

The First China Road and City Exhibition held its opening ceremony at 10:00 AM yesterday inside the newly built venue on Avenue Petain in the French Concession. In addition to Shanghai Mayor Zhang Yuejun, who was delegated by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the National Government to attend, Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting and Industry Minister Kong Xiangxi personally attended and delivered speeches. The details of yesterday's events are recorded as follows:

▲ Attendees The attendees included Zhang Qun, representing Chairman Chiang Kai-shek; Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting; Industry Minister Kong Xiangxi; Vice Minister Zhao Jinqing; Central Committee Member Chu Minyi; President of Labor University Wang Jingqi; Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Yang Nianzu; Cuban Minister General Pédro y Rial; Czech Representative Fei Zheer; members of the China National Roads Construction Association; representatives from various provinces; and thousands of Chinese and foreign guests from all walks of life.

▲ Ceremony Proceedings At 10:20 AM, the opening was announced. Chaired by Zhao Jinqing and emceed by Yang Nianzu, after the ceremony, Chairman Wang Zhengting delivered a speech, followed by Mayor Zhang, representing Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. Industry Minister Kong Xiangxi, Paul, representative of the American Automobile Chamber of Commerce, and Central Committee Member Chu Minyi also spoke. Finally, Cao Yunxiang delivered a response on behalf of the chairman, followed by a photo session and refreshments before the event concluded.

▲ Summary of Wang Zhengting's Speech Distinguished guests, the committee of this association is holding the Road and City Exhibition here today. We are honored to have the presence and guidance of important figures from the Party and the country, as well as esteemed Chinese and foreign gentlemen. This is a great honor for the China Roads Construction Association. The Roads Association has been around for ten years, since its establishment. Over these ten years, the environment has been very difficult and challenging. However, thanks to the efforts of the committee members, the attention of compatriots across the country, and the assistance of foreign friends and overseas Chinese, we have achieved something very gratifying despite the difficulties and hardships. I believe that during the Qing Dynasty, great importance was attached to railways. However, some people at the time only knew to pay attention to railways and considered roads unimportant. It must be understood that while railways are necessary, roads are also needed to support them. Otherwise, how can railways develop? The Premier considered all aspects of transportation. His plan was to build 100,000 kilometers of railways and one million kilometers of roads across the country, as well as dredge canals and establish telephone, wireless, and radio stations. These are all closely related to transportation. Because of inconvenient transportation, all undertakings are hindered. Commerce, industry, and agriculture, no matter what the undertaking, it is very difficult to develop. Therefore, the Premier paid great attention to transportation. So now, which country has the most roads, and which country's people are the happiest? All prosperous urban areas have benefited from convenient road transportation. Wherever a road passes, that place immediately prospers. We must use roads to assist railways to make the Northeast, Northwest, and Southwest prosper. This is a very obvious fact. Moreover, the Northwest and Southwest provinces are currently very poor. If more roads could have been built in the past, they would not be so poor now. From all these aspects, the importance of roads can be imagined. As for construction, railway construction is not easy, but roads can be built anywhere and anytime. Moreover, road construction is much less expensive than railways, but the results are the same. In places without roads, people's lifespans are invisibly shortened. For example, in Shanghai, transportation is convenient. Because the roads are orderly and flat, one can drive a car or streetcar for dozens of miles and reach their destination in an instant. If one walks in a place without roads, or with roads that are rugged and uneven, it takes a lot of effort, and much precious time is wasted. Even if one can use a horse-drawn carriage or other vehicle, one can only travel a short distance in a day. Such is the difficulty in places without roads, and such is the convenience in places with roads. Therefore, the relationship between roads and the country and individuals is of vital interest, and this can be known from this. Our country takes the county as a unit. If every county can do its best to build roads, it is expected that the country will definitely become richer and stronger in a few days. In the future, after there are flat roads to travel around the country, it will only take a few days by car. Recently, Weihaiwei has used a mutual assistance method to build roads since it was taken over. Because the local government saw that farmers had nothing to do in winter and that afternoon work had not yet begun, it gathered many farmers, provided them with tools and materials, and told them to build roads. The people contributed labor, and the government supplied materials. Weihaiwei is now extremely convenient for transportation, and this is the effect. Therefore, the Premier believes that roads are one of the important issues for people's livelihood, so he added a line to the three elements of clothing, food, and housing, and that is what he meant. As for the closest combination between the government and the people, it is the municipal government and the county government. If the municipal and county governments are corrupt, the people will directly suffer. Road construction projects should start from the county, and then do it step by step, and China's roads will have considerable achievements. As for the meaning of today's meeting, on the one hand, it is to express respect, and on the other hand, we also want to ask all sectors to actively assist.

▲ Summary of the Chairman's Welcome Speech The Roads Association has been established for more than ten years. Everyone present should already have a considerable understanding of the effects of past work, so I don't need to elaborate. All undertakings rely on the support of the transportation industry, and the sole purpose of roads is to promote the development of the national transportation industry and plan the construction of the transportation industry. Because the transportation industry is to the country as blood vessels are to the human body. When blood vessels are unblocked, the body is healthy; when transportation is convenient, the country is healthy. If transportation is inconvenient, prosperous areas will be excessively prosperous, and remote areas will eventually be closed off. Various industries have no way to develop. The association has been running around and calling out for ten years, which has aroused the sympathy of the general public, but it has not yet received deep attention. The purpose of this exhibition is to make the general public aware of the importance of the transportation industry, so that the transportation industry can make great progress in the future. This year, China's floods were extremely heavy, with 17 provinces affected and 80 million people affected. From now on, clothing, food, housing, and transportation will all rely on the relief of the transportation industry. Taking food as an example, the eastern provinces of our country have a surplus of soybeans. Because of overproduction and sluggish overseas sales, they are often used as fuel in areas with inconvenient transportation. However, the victims in the Yangtze River basin are starving and have to borrow wheat from the United States, which can be said to be extremely uneconomical. If transportation is convenient, the surplus grain in the eastern provinces can be transported to the starving people, so why should we suppress it to foreigners? China is rich in products, but because of inconvenient transportation, they cannot be transported out. For example, the output of domestic coal is very large, but due to insufficient transportation facilities and weak transportation capacity, the coal used by Shanghai factories is suppressed and supplied to Japan, and manipulated by the Japanese. Furthermore, regarding railway sleepers, the Ministry of Industry once suggested using domestic products in order to promote domestic products. However, after a detailed investigation by the Ministry of Railways, it was found that purchasing foreign sleepers only cost more than two taels of silver, while using domestic products would cost three or four times as much. The reason for this is that there are too few railways built in the country, and transportation is inconvenient, so the cost of transporting them back and forth is really high. There are too many similar facts to mention, and this is a cause for concern. What is most amazing is that if we want to transport goods from Mongolia, Xinjiang, and Tibet into the mainland, we have to use foreign transportation facilities, which is even more painful. Recently, the Russians built a railway near Xinjiang. From the perspective of transportation value, the Russians are not very cost-effective, but because of political relations, the Russians are still actively building this road. It takes dozens of days to get from Nanjing to Xinjiang, but it only takes eight days to get from Siberia to Xinjiang. If our country does not speed up the convenience of transportation in that area, Xinjiang may not belong to us. Therefore, the construction of roads has great significance in terms of economy, politics, and national defense. Sun Yat-sen's plan for 100,000 railways can be said to be far-sighted, and this association is continuing to carry out the plan in accordance with the late Premier's proposition. Furthermore, this flood was also caused by inconvenient transportation, resulting in greater losses and more deaths. In the future, the supply of food, clothing, bedding, agricultural seeds, and agricultural tools will all require a large amount of transportation, so from all perspectives, road construction is really urgent. The biggest source of disease in China today is poverty, and the root cause of poverty is that industry has not been developed. The ancients said that profits were abandoned on the ground, but they did not know how to develop them. But in my opinion, it is not that they do not know how to develop them, but that they cannot develop them because of inconvenient transportation. Even if various land advantages are developed, without convenient transportation tools to transport them out, they are equivalent to waste. Now merchants feel that the transportation capacity is insufficient every day and appeal to the transportation authorities every day. Therefore, I hope that everyone will rise up, open up roads, and build roads, because road construction is a prerequisite for industrial development and a sharp tool for industrial development. There is industry only with transportation, and this is what I dare to assert.

▲ Mayor Zhang's Speech (This is the original manuscript issued by the Mayor) Briefly stated, today is the opening day of the Road and City Exhibition held by the National Roads Association. I am honored to be here on behalf of the Chairman of the National Government. From the perspective of us who are in charge of municipal administration, the construction of administration, in terms of material aspects, the construction of roads is the most important construction. In terms of the implementation of local autonomy, road construction is as important as the investigation of household registration, land surveying, and security. Premier Sun Yat-sen specially marked a "transportation" character besides the characters for clothing, food and housing in the Principle of People’s Livelihood, and listed them side by side with the three problems of clothing, food and housing. Moreover, in the National Construction Strategy and Industrial Plan, he first proposed the development of transportation, believing that transportation is the only tool for developing industry. The reason is that once transportation is revitalized, not only military, political, cultural and other aspects, many difficult problems can be solved, and industry can also be revitalized. Therefore, if a country wants to be rich and strong, it must concentrate its spirit and materials and make special efforts in this way. When we talk about China's construction today, we must pay special attention to this. This is from a positive point of view. From a negative point of view, take this year's flood as an example. I don’t know how many people died because of the flood, and it is even more difficult to count those who were displaced. Floods are of course irresistible, but if road transportation can be more developed than the current situation, the people will not be doomed. Now, because of the unsoundness of various modes of transportation, we cannot adopt a swift and appropriate method to rescue them from danger. This large

Road and City Exhibition Photography (Taken by this newspaper)

Is it an exceptionally sorrowful and painful matter? From the above, it can be seen that transportation issues, in a positive light, greatly influence national construction. However, in a negative light, they even affect the survival of our nation, truly a problem that cannot be ignored. Currently, saving China is the so-called construction of a new China, the only major policy, the only major task, is to strive to develop transportation. The scope of transportation is very broad, including river port issues, railway issues, aviation issues, and road issues. Today is the tenth anniversary of the Road Association and the opening day of the first Road and City Exhibition. Let's first talk about road issues. The functions of roads in various aspects have already been discussed, so I won't go into detail again. Regarding roads, there are distinctions between national roads, provincial roads, city roads, and county roads. National roads are built by the central government, provincial and city roads by provincial and city governments, and county roads by county governments. Only in this way can we divide the work and cooperate to achieve the goal of completion. Taking the city as an example, if urban transportation is very convenient, but transportation from the surrounding rural areas to the city is inconvenient, then urban prosperity will naturally be affected. Therefore, when it comes to road construction, the active improvement of urban transportation is essential, but improving inland transportation and building inland roads is also an urgent matter of fact. During the Qing Dynasty, Beijing was the capital, and at that time, Beijing was the center, repairing the official roads of various provinces, with the so-called "Official Horse North Road," "Official Horse West Road," and "Official Horse South Road." In addition, each province's capital to various places also had official road branches, considered main roads, while many small roads were built between villages and towns, connecting with these main roads, forming a road network. However, since the abolition of the postal station system, road maintenance has gradually stopped. Up to now, our country's road industry is still in its infancy. Fortunately, after the National Revolutionary Army completed the Northern Expedition, the central government followed the will of the Premier and worked hard on political tutelage and construction, implementing local autonomy, and stipulated that during the period of political tutelage, each autonomous unit should construct roads crisscrossing their territories, completing the resolutions of the National Assembly on industrial construction procedures, limited to the end of the 24th year of the Republic of China, that the country must increase and complete 200,000 kilometers of highways. It can be seen that the government and the people's representatives all know the importance of road administration and are working together to promote its realization. Since its establishment, the National Road Association has devoted itself to promoting the development of roads, sparing no effort. The publications it publishes are also very numerous, such as the Municipal Administration Encyclopedia, the Road Encyclopedia, and the Road Monthly, all of which are excellent reference materials for us. Its plans and contributions to China's road and municipal administration can be said to be very sophisticated and great. When constructing roads in various parts of the country, the Road Association's assistance in terms of talent and planning is also very significant. Now, it has also organized this Municipal Exhibition, the main purpose of which is to promote the development of both road and municipal aspects, and it happens to be held in this city, so this city will naturally benefit more. In addition to representing the Chairman of the National Government in extending greetings, I can also, on behalf of the municipal authorities, extend a message to the Road Association and wish you all the best in your efforts.

▲Kong Xiangxi's speech (excerpt) Generally speaking, the human environment changes due to needs. The roads in various parts of northern China are very wide, ranging from forty to sixty feet. The roads in southern China are very narrow because there are more dry roads in the north and more waterways in the south, so southerners mostly focus on waterways. But now the environment has changed, and current transportation is very different from the past. With cars and trains, what used to take several days now only takes a few hours. There is an ancient Chinese saying, "The King's way is vast, the King's way is smooth," meaning that the road must be wide and flat. Under the leadership of the Kuomintang, promoting local autonomy is the most important thing. There is also the Principle of People's Livelihood advocated by the Kuomintang. The Principle of People's Livelihood is the most important point of the Premier's Three Principles of the People. Building roads is also an element of the Principle of People's Livelihood. Recently, an officer returning from Jiangxi said that there are no good roads in Jiangxi, so it is very difficult to suppress bandits because without good roads, the Red bandits hide everywhere and attack the National Army. If there were many good roads in Jiangxi, transportation would be convenient, and the work of suppressing bandits would be much more convenient. In addition to roads, we must also pay attention to waterways, such as the Grand Canal, which starts from Tianjin and extends to the Jiangnan area. In the past, it was dug by hand, but recently, due to the emphasis on trains, the river channel has become silted, so there was such a big flood in northern Jiangsu this year. Therefore, in addition to paying attention to roads, we should also pay attention to waterways. Recently, the Northeast Liaoning Minsheng Factory manufactured a cargo car, which can be said to be the first self-made car in China. Although the raw materials are not entirely domestically produced, according to the latest news, the factory is now trying its best to improve manufacturing. This is also something worth our attention. Everyone knows about Henry Ford, the inventor of the car. When he started his research, many people said he was a fool, researching machines on an empty lot next to a hotel every day, and eating in the hotel as well. When the research was about to succeed, Ford asked the hotel owner if he wanted to buy shares in the car company. The hotel owner shook his head and did not agree. Later, the company prospered, and one yuan of capital yielded ten thousand yuan in profit. Therefore, the hotel owner complained to himself every day, deeply regretting that he did not buy shares in the car company before, otherwise he would also be a big tycoon. As for after the success of the car, not only did Ford personally make a fortune, but the United States also benefited from it. Therefore, I hope that everyone can develop roads with the spirit of Ford, then the results will be very promising. With the development of transportation, world harmony is also easier to achieve. (Recorded by Bingxun Quick Recording Agency, Guan Jingbo)

▲Chu Minyi's speech (excerpt) The relationship between roads and the national livelihood has been explained in detail by Chairman Wang, Chairman Kong, and Mayor Zhang, so there is no need to repeat it. However, the inconvenience of transportation in China is a real fact. I just returned from Xinjiang three days ago. In the past, it took at least a hundred days to go to Xinjiang, and the roads were uneven, making travel very difficult. But by taking a mountain-climbing car, it only takes thirty days to reach it. However, I still have a feeling, which is that to go to a place within our own country, we have to go through a foreign country. This is very sad and heartbreaking. For example, to go to Xinjiang, we have to go through the Siberian Railway; to go to Yunnan, we have to go through Annam. Therefore, we must resolutely and actively promote road construction, and then political, economic, and other kinds of problems will have the hope of development. This is my point of view to share with everyone.

▲Li Yichun's account of the process of creating a car. The National Road and City Exhibition opened yesterday. More than a hundred cars of various sizes and types were displayed at the exhibition, but only one of them was made in China. However, this car is the most attention-grabbing to Chinese and foreigners. This car is a product of the Liaoning Minsheng Factory and was created by Li Yichun, the director of the Liaoning Mortar Factory. For the opening of this exhibition, Mr. Li specially transported this car to be displayed and sent Mr. Zhang Yunting to participate in the conference. The following is an excerpt from Mr. Li's own account of the process of creating the car and a description of the current situation of the factory: (1) Preliminary test: Heavy-duty trucks are very much needed at the moment. Mr. Zhang Hanqing specially allocated more than 40,000 yuan from the remaining funds of the Mortar Factory to purchase machinery, materials, and research purposes. In August of the eighteenth year, famous single-part vehicles were shipped from the United States, and the factory assembled them to complete them for preliminary testing. Later, the purchased Releigh car was disassembled, and its important parts and easily damaged parts were redesigned and remanufactured. This was the beginning of the factory's manufacturing of cars. (2) Manufacturing plan: The heavy-duty trucks that the factory originally planned to manufacture are divided into two types: (1) Type 55, with a load capacity of about two tons; (2) Type 100, with a load capacity of three tons. Type 55 is usually referred to as small and Type 100 as large. The small car is best suited for the existing roads in Chinese cities and towns. The entire body is manufactured by the factory. Except for a few single parts, such as engine rear axle electrical devices and tires, which are either more complex to manufacture or lack raw materials, it is difficult to immediately manufacture them ourselves in practice, so we temporarily entrust foreign specialized factories to manufacture them according to the drawings made by our factory. All other parts are designed and manufactured by our factory. The large car is specially designed for driving on rural and poor roads. Although the car's speed is not very high, it is very useful for loading heavy and bulky goods for long-distance transportation. The manufacturing method is the same as that of the small car, but the tires are changed to semi-soft rubber. Because air tires are not suitable for use on rural roads, if they are specially designed for use on city roads, it is of course better to install air tires. The installation of tires can be changed at will, with the goal of being suitable. It is not fixed. The first batch of manufacturing now needs to increase the weight, so it has been changed to Type 75. The estimated annual production volume is 100 Type 75s and 55 Type 100s. (3) Enthusiastic promotion: The factory's capital is purely allocated by the Northeast Frontier Defense Army Commander's Office. In February of the eighteenth year, more than 43,000 yuan was allocated from the surplus funds of the Mortar Factory to serve as the testing fee for preparing civilian goods. The foundation of the factory was laid here. In the nineteenth year, the test production was successful, and preparations were made to open the factory. Later, the factory was allocated 750,000 yuan in national currency as the capital for starting manufacturing. Commander Zhang has always spared no effort in the construction of the country and the promotion of industry. At a time when the country is in trouble and the financial resources of the eastern provinces are sometimes stretched, Mr. Hanqing is still able to do everything possible to find ways in addition to political and military affairs. (4) Minsheng Factory: The Mortar Factory is purely a machine for manufacturing weapons and had no plans to create commercial goods at first. Since the unification of the north and south in the eighteenth year of the Republic of China and the reduction of military equipment, there has been a trend throughout the country to strive for material construction. The Liaoning Mortar Factory then had an attached Minsheng Factory, with the aim of developing industry and supplying civilian goods, and the business of manufacturing automobiles, greenhouse materials, and various leathers. (5) Selecting personnel: The factory attaches great importance to technical talents. At the beginning of its establishment, it hired American technician Myers as an engineer. Chu talents are used, and Yichun

Liaoning Minsheng Factory Self-made Car

It was not a matter of choice. In addition to manufacturing, a small number of foreigners were hired. All other important staff members are graduates of domestic and foreign universities and specialized departments. The use of people is completely based on qualifications, experience, and ability as the standard. The factory currently has 30 staff members and 177 workers. (6) Exchange of knowledge: Many of the factory's important staff members have joined the American Society of Automotive Engineers as members, in order to exchange knowledge. Written introductions, correspondence, and discussions are especially important. Therefore, the factory's staff members can obtain information about any new inventions, new creations, and drawing designs in the American automobile manufacturing industry earlier as members, and the samples and explanations obtained are also more detailed. The factory also has considerable contact with automobile companies such as Ford, General Motors, International, and Spyk, and plans to send the factory's workers to American factories every year in the near future to practice in order to seek further education. (7) First batch of products: Since the successful production of the first domestically produced car manufactured by the factory in May of this year, we have been manufacturing large batches of products according to the model to meet social needs. As the quality of the first batch of products is closely related to the factory's reputation and credit, the factory is working hard to be cautious and strive for perfection. It is now expected that the first batch will produce 45 Type 75 heavy-duty trucks. Most of the parts for the entire car have been completed, and they can be manufactured into cars as soon as they are complete. It is expected that they will be able to meet the people of the country in two months. (8) Low price: The value of the new car manufactured by the factory has been calculated, and the result is that it is not only not higher than other vehicles of the same level, but is actually lower. This is because foreign wages are ten times higher, and the cost of transporting parts and materials is particularly low compared to the shipping costs and insurance costs of transporting the entire car. Moreover, when paying import and export tariffs, the tax rate for transporting the entire car is several times higher than that for transporting parts and materials, which includes labor costs. These are the two main reasons for the low price.

▲Bauer discusses the relationship between roads and automobiles. Mr. Bauer, representative of the American Automotive Industry Chamber of Commerce, gave a speech, saying, "It is a great pleasure to be here with you today. But we must know that this Road and City Exhibition is not the starting point of road construction. Your country has already made progress in this regard. What is needed now is the connection of various roads. If we open our eyes and examine your country's road map, we can understand that if the existing lines are slightly

Page 18

extended, a complete road network can be obtained. This is also the responsibility of all gentlemen present and will rank your country among the civilized countries with good roads. The purpose of this association is not limited to this. Road builders are for the convenience of automobiles, and automobiles are machines. Therefore, the best way to repair roads is also with machines. We often say that labor is sacred, but we must also use achievement as the standard. Using machines can make labor have a better effect. What ordinary people say that the status of labor is harmed by machines is actually a specious argument. From the perspective of the workers' interests, it is better to complete the roads quickly. According to statistics from various countries, even if machines are used to build roads, three-quarters of the funds are distributed to labor. However, the effect of road repair is even greater. According to statistics, the United States has developed roads and convenient transportation. Therefore, every six cars can provide one person with work. If China uses machines to build roads and completes various lines as soon as possible, it can also achieve this goal. By then, business will prosper and the people will have more opportunities to work. Automobile sales, repairs, driving, gas stations, hostels, food stores, etc., can all be operated. Canada earns 300 million yuan annually from tourists entering the country from the United States. The great benefits of this can be seen here. China has many elegant scenery and places famous in history, which can also be emulated. Nanjing and Hangzhou can also attract foreign funds invisibly. If the points passed by the current Beijing-Hangzhou Road can be directly connected with Shanghai, the nearby residents will benefit even more. This can develop resources and promote commerce. The automobile transportation industry itself is also very important. In the United States, the annual revenue is 80 billion gold yuan, second only to the total turnover of food. If China has good road administration, it can encourage automobile transportation and reap this huge profit. Road maintenance costs can also provide people with work. From the perspective of the people's interests, it is better to complete all roads as soon as possible than to build them slowly. After the roads are completed, there are many maintenance affairs that can accommodate a large number of engineers and workers. Uruguay in South America builds a small house every mile of road to house two road repairmen. If China follows this, the staff members of the highway bureaus in various provinces will have no worries about work opportunities. Furthermore, the use of machinery to develop roads on a large scale is an element of a country's progress. Fortunately, gentlemen, please remember this. Today, various provinces in China, such as Jiangsu and Anhui, are suffering from floods. Road construction is also one of the relief methods, as it can make use of disaster victims to work and provide relief. Moreover, with convenient transportation, food transportation and population relocation are faster. If a disaster occurs again in the future, it will still be easier to deal with. The method of building national roads is also quite simple. Counting them, there are only four items: (1) It is necessary to enable people to have the ability to purchase and use automobiles. For example, reducing taxes can reduce the cost of purchasing them. (2) Then, as there are more automobiles, the registration fees and gasoline donations can compensate for the government's tax reductions. (3) Then, the revenue from this tax must be independent and used exclusively for highway loan interest and fundraising. Fourth, private construction companies should be allowed to bid to build roads and municipal construction projects planned by the government. China today already has the best road engineers. If these can be implemented, new tools can be obtained to complete the transportation of this great country." Shanghai, September 12, 1931.

Municipal Party Headquarters Convenes First Propaganda Meeting

Resolutions on important cases such as Guangdong affairs, flood disaster, and anti-Japanese movement

The Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters convened the first municipal propaganda meeting of this session yesterday afternoon at 1:00 p.m., attended by propaganda committee members from various districts of the city. Wu Xiu chaired the meeting. After the meeting began with formalities, the chairman first reported, followed by reports from the propaganda committee members of various districts on the recent work status. Then, the proposed motions were discussed: (A) The national flood disaster is serious, with many victims and a wide disaster area. How should we awaken the city's people to enthusiastically raise funds for emergency relief to provide assistance? Resolutions: (1) Each district should organize disaster relief propaganda teams to give speeches. (2) Periodicals in each district should publish as much information as possible about the tragic situation in the disaster area and commend individuals or organizations who are enthusiastic about disaster relief. (3) A request should be submitted to the Municipal Executive Committee to strictly order all party members in the city to tighten their belts and work hard to assist in disaster relief as an example. (B) In the autumn of national crisis and disaster, Guangdong actually dared to take risks, advocating rebellion and claiming military power, and recently sent troops to the border of Hunan, willing to be the head of the rebels. How should we respond to this serious situation? Resolutions: (1) In the name of this meeting, send a telegram to the Guangdong authorities to give a final warning. (2) Send a telegram to all provinces in the country, explaining the sinister intentions of Guangdong's dispatch of troops to invade Hunan. If peace cannot be achieved, we should fight and ask for a united advocacy to uphold justice. (3) Request the central government to stop Guangdong's military actions. If they do not realize their mistakes, they should be ordered to suppress them to punish the ringleaders and save the country from disaster. (C) Celebrating National Day. Resolution: Follow the orders of the central government and persuade various organizations, schools, and all citizens of this city to transfer the expenses of banquets, entertainment, and lanterns during the celebration to disaster relief funds. Temporary motion: The work of the Anti-Japanese Association has seemed to decline recently. It is proposed to submit a request to the Municipal Executive Committee for strict supervision to encourage public morale. Resolution: Passed. After the discussion, the meeting was adjourned.

City Boy Scouts Donated Along the Way Yesterday

Opening the Box Today

The citywide donation organized by the Shanghai City Boy Scout Flood Disaster Relief Committee was held yesterday. The following is a summary of the donation situation:

▲Police Misunderstanding: All Boy Scout troops started donating in their designated areas from 6:00 a.m. yesterday. The Chinese and Western people along the way were moved by the young children who worked tirelessly to beg for disaster relief and were willing to donate generously. Unexpectedly, in the Nanshi, Zhabei, and Pudong areas, due to improper procedures, the police interfered. For example, one or two donation boxes and symbols of the Boy Scouts of Shanghai Middle School were taken away by the police. As a result, the donation teams in the Chinese area reported to the donation and relief association that the police were interfering. After receiving the report, the vice captains of the donation, Wang Gang and Leng Xueqiao, rushed to the municipal government and the emergency relief association of various provinces to request assistance. The municipal government approved the order to the municipal public security bureau to order all branches to stop interfering at 12:00 noon. Although the original state was restored once, it was eventually blocked by the police after 3:00 p.m. Due to this small misunderstanding, the donation results were slightly affected. This is truly unfortunate for the disaster victims.

▲City Games Influence: The Girls' Physical Education School, which has Boy Scouts in this city, originally wanted to participate in the donation in full, but due to the city games competition and service, more than 400 people participated, resulting in a reduction in donation power. This is truly another misfortune for the disaster victims.

▲Organize a Special Donation Team: In view of the above unfortunate situation, the association was deeply concerned that the donation amount would not be large, so it organized a special donation team, which was led by the 50th, 65th, 121st, and 270th troops, and Boy Scout service members. The time was extended to 2:00 a.m. It is hoped that with the addition of this new force, the results will be considerable.

▲Indian Police Assist in Donation: A respectable Indian patrolman No. 181 stationed at the intersection of Dama Road and Henan Road saw the donation situation and took one yuan in foreign currency and put it into the Boy Scout donation box. His heart of generosity is truly admirable.

▲Boys and Girls Commendable: A seven-year-old girl in a mansion on Chongqing Road specially took out more than 200 copper coins she had saved when she saw the donation and put them into the donation box. There was also a barefoot boy, about twelve years old. When Wang Gang, the deputy commander of the donation team, was patrolling to the New World Palace Grand Theater, he suddenly asked Wang, "Sir, what are you doing today?" Wang immediately told him that the city's Boy Scouts were raising funds for the flood disaster in various provinces. The boy replied, "I have a dime of silver, and I would like to use it as a relief fund. I wonder if I can be accepted?" Wang saw that he was young and ambitious, so he granted his request and ordered him to put it into a Boy Scout donation box. The above two children, only about ten years old, were willing to give generously. Although the amount is small, it is truly commendable.

▲Old Man Promotes and Assists in Donation: An elderly man, because he had no money to donate, shouted loudly to help the Boy Scouts promote. His enthusiasm for doing good deeds is truly admirable and praiseworthy.

▲Opening the Box in Public Today: The donation committee has scheduled to hand in the donations at the Moore Memorial Church on Sanma Road at 9:00 a.m. today. Please ask representatives from various agencies to open the box. It is reported that Mayor Zhang Yuejun has sent Mr. Wu Bilai to attend the meeting to supervise.

Flood Disaster Relief Society Resolves to Issue Charitable Champagne

▲A total of 100,000 tickets worth 1 million yuan

▲A total of 800,000 yuan in prizes

▲More than 50,000 tickets were recognized on the spot

▲The remaining tickets will be distributed and sold by various newspapers

▲Date: October 25th

The members of the flood disaster relief associations of various provinces, Qian Xinzhi, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, etc., held a tea party yesterday afternoon at 3:00 p.m. at Yiyuan to entertain people from all walks of life. On the spot, it was resolved to issue 100,000 charitable champagne tickets. More than 50,000 tickets were recognized by the initiators on the spot. The details are recorded below:

▲Attendees: Yesterday's attendees included Zhang Qun, Wang Xiaolai, Zheng Yuxiu, Qian Xinzhi, Lin Kanghou, Mu Ouchu, Wu Yunzhai, Wen Lanting, Wang Yiting, Wu Zhihao, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Shi Liangcai, Zhang Zhuping, Wang Boqi, Li Zushen, Huang Boqiao, Yu Hongjun, Xu Yongzuo, Chu Minyi, and hundreds of others.

▲Tea Party Situation: Mayor Zhang, the chairman, first reported, saying, "This flood has spread to sixteen provinces, with tens of millions of victims. All walks of life in Shanghai have tried their best to help. However, only more than 700,000 yuan has been raised so far, which is far from enough for distribution. Therefore, the women's community has prepared tea parties and dances, and Mr. Zhang Xiaolin and Du Yuesheng have also planned to issue champagne tickets. Mr. Zhang will report on the various measures."

▲Mr. Zhang's Report: Zhang Xiaolin then reported, saying, "The issuance of champagne tickets totals 100,000 tickets. The first prize is 448,000 yuan, and the second prize is 128,000 yuan. Based on the previous champagne issuance results, they can be sold out immediately. I hope that everyone present will advocate for them and sell at least 100 tickets per person." Wang Xiaolai and Lin Kanghou then expressed their opinions.

▲Si Berlin Discusses: Si Berlin, Chairman of the Board of Directors of Yiyuan, Director of the China Foreign Relief Association, and Member of the National Government Flood Relief Committee, expressed his opinion, saying, "I also sympathize with the disaster relief. I agree with the champagne matter, but the income is limited, so it is necessary to expand the scale and raise funds urgently. I have a plan that can raise 10 million to 20 million yuan in relief funds, which can be drafted in one or two weeks. I will ask everyone to discuss it at that time and ask for your assistance." Zheng Yuxiu then expressed his opinion. It was then proposed to show a flood disaster film, but since the equipment was not brought, Li Zushen, who went to Hankou for disaster relief, reported on the disaster situation, etc. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 p.m.

▲Champagne Measures: It was decided to issue 100,000 champagne tickets. One first prize of 448,000 yuan, one second prize of 128,000 yuan, one third prize of 64,000 yuan, and other small prizes totaling 160,000 yuan. The champagne race will be held on October 25th. Each ticket is 10 yuan, totaling 1 million yuan. After deducting the prizes, there will be more than 200,000 yuan left, which will all be used for disaster relief funds. All expenses, etc., will be borne by the China Jockey Club. When claiming the prize, tickets are recognized, not people. The prize money can be collected from the bank with the ticket without any discount.

▲On-site Recognition: Yesterday, more than 50,000 tickets were recognized on the spot. The remaining 40,000 tickets are expected to be sold out immediately when they are issued. It has been decided that Shen Bao, News, Times, Current Affairs News, Minguo Daily, and Continental News will distribute and sell them on behalf of the six newspapers. The tickets will be printed and issued within ten days.

▲ Attention to Autumn and Spring Planting in Disaster Areas. The National Government Flood Relief Committee, considering that the water levels in the disaster areas along the Yangtze River are gradually receding, and in preparation for planting this autumn and next spring, has approved the application of the committee's consultant, Mr. Baker, and sent a letter to the civil affairs departments of the provincial governments of Hunan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Jiangsu yesterday, requesting them to investigate the approximate amount of seeds needed in the disaster areas to facilitate work. The original letter is recorded as follows: "Dear Sirs, in order to plan for the planting of spring rice seeds in various disaster areas, it is urgently necessary to investigate the approximate seed requirements of each province. It is requested that you write to the officials of the affected provinces and ask them to investigate and report the details for reference." The relevant points to be investigated are listed below, and we request you to investigate in detail and reply promptly so that we can inform them accordingly. The details are as follows: (1) How many acres of land have been affected by the disaster in your province? (2) How many acres of land can be planted when the water recedes this autumn? (3) What kind of grains can be planted there? (4) Are the seeds stored in your province sufficient? (5) What kind of seeds are lacking? (6) How much of what kind of grain seeds are lacking? (7) When is the latest planting time? (8) Is there a shortage of japonica rice seeds during spring planting? (9) What kind of grains and in what quantity does your province still need?

Shanghai Authorities to Transfer Kidnapping Ring Leader Liang Faxiu from Tianjin

Shuai Zhongping, the bandit who kidnapped Lu Shaotang, was arrested in Beiping and transferred to Shanghai. After interrogation by the Special District Court, he was sentenced to death. Shuai refused to accept the verdict and filed an appeal. It is now learned that the leader of the kidnapping gang, Liang Faxiu, is hiding in the Tianjin Second Special District. He is also a former Qing official, rumored to have held military positions such as commander. The local public security bureau dispatched armed detectives to arrest Liang the day before yesterday. During interrogation at the public security bureau, he confessed to making a living solely by kidnapping, having kidnapped wealthy individuals more than 40 times, with ransoms exceeding 100,000 yuan each time. He purchased more than a dozen properties in Shanghai to hide the kidnapped individuals and over a hundred cars for kidnapping purposes. He also has many followers. Currently detained at the Public Security Bureau, the Public Concession Police Department has investigated and reported the case to the Special District Court, preparing a document to send detectives to Tianjin to bring him back to Shanghai for trial.

Labor Dispute at Jingwei Silk Weaving Company Involves Lawsuit

Management Disagrees with Arbitration Decision,

Files Lawsuit Seeking Annulment

The Shanghai Jingwei Silk Weaving Company on Baoding Road, Hongkou, employs many workers but rarely experiences labor unrest. On April 21st of this year, after discovering that 19 bolts of silk produced were defective, resulting in inferior quality, the company dismissed the workers responsible. Other workers expressed support for those dismissed and took leave on the 26th. The factory, considering this disruptive, dismissed several more workers. As a result, ten workers dismissed in two rounds, including Xu Xilin, Yu Aye, Shen Feitang, Wang Zhongrui, Qian Zhangnan, Song Qiwen, Shi Agen, He Alin, He Ashi, and Pan Yingzhou, jointly petitioned the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for mediation, which failed. The labor representatives then petitioned the Municipal Government for arbitration. Approved by the Municipal Government, Guo 　, Tao Baichuan, Pang Shurong, Zhang Yaoming, and Ma Jiliang were appointed to form an arbitration committee, with Guo as the chairman. They summoned both labor and management for questioning. According to the management, the workers' poor performance violated factory rules and their leave and coercion disrupted order, justifying the dismissal. However, the labor representatives claimed that the defective silk was not produced by the dismissed workers and that there was no disruptive behavior. After discussion between Chairman Guo and all members of the committee, it was concluded that the reasons stated by the management were insufficient, and the facts presented could not be definitively proven, indicating a failure to comply with labor laws in the dismissal of the workers, which was deemed inappropriate. The decision was that Xu Xilin and the other nine workers should be reinstated. After receiving the decision, the management, through their representative lawyer Hong Shanghao, filed a petition with the First Special District District Court based on existing labor laws, seeking to annul the arbitration committee's decision. Yesterday morning, Judge Guo Shouyi held a hearing. Many of the workers' representatives were absent. Lawyer Hong stated the reasons why the management could not comply with the arbitration decision. Judge Guo, believing that a peaceful resolution was best for the case, advised both parties to go outside and negotiate. Labor disputes have occurred frequently in recent years, and most have been resolved through mediation. This is the first time a case has gone to court.

Higher Second Branch Yesterday Burned Reactionary Books

The Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court, from January to June of this year, has accumulated a large number of reactionary books, newspapers, leaflets, and other publications confiscated as a result of reactionary cases it has handled. With the approval of the Ministry of Justice, Director Xu of the court and Chief Prosecutor Wang ordered them to be burned publicly. Yesterday afternoon, the court selected an open space in the Bao'antang, south of the court, as the burning site, ordering public servants to transport the publications and dispatching court police to maintain order. Several prosecutors also attended the site for supervision. At around 3:00 PM, with all procedures completed, the fire was started, and each item was identified and thrown into the flames. By dusk, all items had been reduced to ashes.

Russian Teenager Commits Suicide in Fukushima Garden

Building number 114, Jin Shenfu Road, French Concession, is the residence of Fukushima, the Japanese general manager of Mitsui & Co. on Sichuan Road. For security, Fukushima hired two Indian watchmen. Yesterday morning, at around 6:00 AM, before the two Indian watchmen had gotten up, they suddenly heard two gunshots from the garden behind the residence. The two watchmen were immediately startled and followed the sound to the side of the driveway in the garden. They found a young Russian man lying on the ground, groaning, with a gun in his right hand. There was a clear trail of blood on the left side of his chest. The two watchmen were terrified and immediately ran to inform their employer, Fukushima, who telephoned the police station. The police chief ordered detectives to investigate. It was determined to be a suicide, and the man was immediately taken to the nearby Guangci Hospital. Due to the critical nature of the injuries, he was unconscious upon arrival at the hospital. It was reported that the Russian man's name was Hodireff, 25 years old, and he was currently working as a bodyguard for the Hong family at number 17 Julai Road. The reason for his sudden suicide is suspected to be due to special circumstances.

It is said that the Russian man was previously an officer in the military. Recently, his wife had found another lover and secretly took their two-year-old daughter with her, disappearing without a trace, leading to his despair and suicide. It is also reported that before taking his own life, he wrote a letter to the director of a certain Russian club, explaining his indignation.

World Famous Swimmer Comes to Shanghai

Mr. Madegan

Mr. Madegan, the world-famous swimmer, arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday. A reporter from a local foreign newspaper visited him at his residence and inquired about his experiences in detail. According to Mr. Madegan, he has been making a living from this for 34 years. His father was a renowned athlete. When Madegan was young, his father would throw him into the river and guide him with an oar, teaching him swimming. In 1897, with the help of a friend, he became a high-diving swimmer at the New York Park Amusement Association. Since then, he has traveled to various countries, earning many accolades. Many great men from various countries have appreciated his skills. He once wanted to retire to enjoy his remaining years, but his wife said that with his strength, he could still work for ten years. But in ten years, he would be a 67-year-old man. If he could still swim in a pool, he would be very lucky. It would be impossible for him to jump from a 105-foot-high ladder into a bucket of water only five feet deep. When he first learned this skill, he jumped from a height of 65 feet into a bucket of water nine feet deep, which he already found remarkable. He never expected to achieve a height of 105 feet with a bucket of water only five feet deep. The amount of water in the bucket cannot be reduced any further because the force of jumping from a 105-foot ladder into the water is at least four and a half feet. Only five inches of water are left to ensure safety. If his eyesight is not accurate when jumping, or if something goes wrong, he will not clear the bucket, and if he hits the bottom of the bucket, his body will be shattered. It is said that his visit to China this time coincides with the Chinese flood disaster, so he is very willing to perform his skills once for free, with the proceeds going to flood relief.

Nameless Woman on the Xinning Steamer Jumps into the Sea

The Municipal Public Security Bureau Investigates Family Members

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau sent a letter to this newspaper yesterday stating: "Dear Sirs, according to a letter from the Qingdao Municipal Public Security Bureau, Huang Yinsheng, a comprador of the Taikoo Yanghang Xinning steamer, reported to the bureau on August 24th of this year that when the ship arrived in Qingdao from Shanghai today, the steward serving the guests discovered during inspection that a Chinese female passenger in the first-class cabin was missing. A letter was found in the female passenger's cabin, which was the suicide note of the female passenger (anonymous). Upon examining the meaning of the suicide note, it was learned that the female passenger had committed suicide by jumping into the sea. The items were handed over to the British Consulate in Qingdao for forwarding. The Third Branch of this Bureau also reported the same situation. While the investigation was underway, the comprador submitted a telegram from Pan Peiqing of the Shanghai Cangzhou Hotel asking whether Xu Sichao in cabin number ten had arrived safely in Qingdao and requesting a telegram in reply. This Bureau immediately sent a quick mail to Pan Peiqing with the details of the incident, a copy of the deceased's suicide note, and a list of the items, instructing him to reply quickly to clarify the truth. Now, the Municipal Post Office has returned the original letter sent by this Bureau to Pan Peiqing with the endorsement 'Addressee has left, undeliverable.' Although the deceased's name has been identified, her place of origin, address, whether she has family members or relatives, and the reasons for her suicide remain unclear. In addition to recording the case and reporting it to the Qingdao Municipal Government for record, we are sending a copy of the deceased's suicide note and a list of items to your bureau, hoping you will investigate and verify. Therefore, since the nameless woman who jumped into the sea has no address, it is impossible to find and notify her family members. We are specially requesting your newspaper to publish this in the news column so that her family members will be informed to go to Qingdao to claim the belongings."
